%   The Hungarian corpus used in Gervain and Guevara (under review).
%   The corpus contains the child-directed adult utterances of the Hungarian subcorpora of the CHILDES database. The corpus was processed for the purposes of the study. The processing is described in detail in Gervain and Guevara (under review).
%   The double characters of Hungarian orthography (cs, dz, gy etc.) were replaced by numbers as follows. All other characters are used as in standard Hungarian. Note, however, that the corpus was phonotypically transcribed, so the characters indicate phonemes, i.e. pronunciation, not actual graphemes.
%   1 = cs, unvoiced post alveolar affricate, as in csak 'only' (like English ch in church)
%   2 = dz, voiced alveolar affricate, as in madzag 'rope, string' (like English ds in Leeds)
%   3 = dzs, voiced postalveolar affricate, as in dzsungel 'jungle' (like English j in jungle) 
%   4 = gy, voiced palatal affricate, as in gyár 'factory' (similar to the palatal prnunciation of d in duty)
%   5 = ny, palatal nasal, as in nyár 'summer' (similar to the palatal prnunciation of n in new)
%   6 = sz, voiceless alveolar fricative, as in szem 'eye' (like English s in see)
%   7 = ty, voiceless palatal affricate, as in tyúk 'hen' (similar to the palatal prnunciation of t in tube)
%   8 = zs, voiced postalveolar fricative, as in zseb 'pocket' (similar to ge in the US pronunciation of garage)

%   0 indicates utterance boundaries. These were inserted for easy of exposition. They were deleted for the purposes of the statistical analysis.

%   Boundary notation:
%   UB = utterance boundary
%   WB = word boundary
%   MB = morpheme boundary
%   WI = word innternal (i.e. no boundary)

%   Publications using this corpus should cite:
Gervain, Judit & Guevara Erra, Ramon. (under review). "The Statistical Signature of Morphosyntax: A Study of Hungarian and Italian Infant-Directed Speech".
